<userid>105698011657286419498< /userid>< review>
So many nooks and crannies you are sure to find your comfortable hangout spot. Rigoberto Menchu on the terrace level is the hidden gem. What looks like a comfortable fireplace lounge really goes up 5 stories to the inside of one of the pyramids. You can not tell what might be going on up there from the bottom level. Several areas have phone charging stations. The game room in the basement is always a good getaway. The depot has live music two nights a week and get connected to the calendar of events to stay connected to campus.< /review>

<rating>4</rating>< review>
When I crave dumplings and skewers in Fremont, this is my go-to place. The dumplings and lamb skewers (eat them hot!) are absolutely 5 star quality. My family and I ordered the Northeastern Style Salad and beef noodle soup as well. I thought that the Northeastern Style Salad's noodles were a bit thick and I guess I was expecting it to be more flavorful.<//review>

<Text>**updated Jan 2019. This place is more prepared now and the service is reasonably fast/friendly. The portion is good enough for adults and price didn't go up at all comparing to a year ago.

A new dumpling place replaced the old fashion house. The dumpling here isn't bad although they are small considering the price. The skin is a little thick but not too difficult to chew. The stuffing is nice and they come with sauce (soy sauce and garlic slices).
They are still in soft opening mode and it's really really slow. We waited for over 40 mins for 2 orders of dumpling and therefore, 2 star.
I'll update the review later if I see improvement.<//Text>< Rate>

<Review>Visited on Sunday 9/17. A thing to keep in mind is the restaurant is still in "Soft Opening" as of the writing of this review.

I visited with one other person and I honestly do not have any complaints. The staff was very helpful in letting us know about the menu, and the food took around 10 minutes.

We ordered the shrimp/chive/egg dumplings and it was very tasty, with very thin and soft skin. We also had the cucumber (was lightly picked and had cilantro and garlic), and the seaweed which was very tasty.

<text>The Snug is remeniscent of a speakeasy. Tucked in around the side of the main stretch off R St, you'll walk through a large set of wooden doors into the dim but bustling bar. The Snug is decorated with classic wallpaper, lounge chairs, wall sconces, and a warthog. Despite it being busy, the bartenders are efficient. We had drinks in hand minutes after arriving. < Text>
Very nice!  It's tough to pull off, but the atmosphere here is upscale and simultaneously unpretentious.  The bartenders are extremely hospitable, and helpful if you're unsure, to guide you toward a drink you'll love.  I went in with the goal of trying some irish whiskeys.  There's one I really love, and i wanted to see if I could find another.  The barkeep on duty that night suggested 2, ond poured me samples.  One knocked my socks off.  Having solved one mystery, I tried something from the mixed menu.  Very tasty, and reasonably priced.  I had 2 while reading a novel.  Looks like the place is generally frequented by members of the state workforce who have to wear dress shoes.< /Text>

<gmap_id>0x80e83713553007d9:0x98d0d251c29707a8</gmap_id><name>Kailey Noel-Rae< /name><user>106208265100199035857</user>< Rating>

<Response>None< /Response><Text>Dr. Lanzon and his staff are excellent - knowledgeable, trustworthy and caring are the three words I would use to describe their services. I would highly recommend Dr. Lanzon for any dental work that you may need.

To give you and idea of what I experienced for my procedure, here is a summary:

My teeth, mostly due to genetics and a love of sugar, were starting to get past the point where they could be saved and rather than keep fixing them one at time for the rest of my life, I made the decision to remove them and replace them with upper and lower implants. This decision was not an easy one but one that was necessary.

With the help of Dr. Lanzon and Dr. Oquist (my dentist), we worked out a treatment and replacement plan that would have the most chance of success. Nothing is guaranteed with this type of major dental work but, after several consultations with Dr. Lanzon, I was confident that he could provide the expertise needed for this "upgrade". And I already knew and trusted that my dentist, who would be coordinating the final appliances (teeth) that would be attached to the implants, was well versed in the process as well. So even though I had no idea what to expect, they did - and their confidence helped to prepare me for what was to come.

First step in the process was to remove my lower teeth, but because I was unsure of how I would react to the removal of my teeth, I decided to just remove half and let the necessary bone grafts become established. In looking back, I should have taken their recommendation to have them all removed at once but to their credit they worked with my two-step plan so that I would feel more comfortable. It turned out that they were right, and that my decision resulted in having to endure one extra healing process (about two months) that could have been avoided had I taken their advice. So the lesson learned here was to accept their advice!!

A few months after this first removal of teeth, I had the remaining lower teeth removed. After pulling the teeth, five implant posts were added. Then a temporary fixed denture was fabricated to fit the posts and attached. All of this was done in a one day session and I was under anesthesia for the entire time so I had no idea what was happening and no pain. When I left his office that day I had new bottom teeth, temporary but impossible to tell that they were not real.

The healing process was brutal for the first few days with lots of rest and enough pain pills to survive. I could not eat normally so it was milk shakes, smoothies, applesauce and mashed potatoes for about a week, and then small sliced up food that could be soft chewed for the next two weeks. After that it was back to normal for food but still staying on the less chewy side of foods so that the healing and strengthening process could continue. Six months later, I had the upper teeth removed, five implant posts were added and then a temporary denture fabricated and attached. Same healing process although the upper implant procedure caused much more swelling than the lower but recovery time was about the same.

Six months after this, we started the process of fabricating the permanent teeth to fit the now sturdy posts. It took a few tweaks to get the teeth just right but once completed they were attached to the posts and have been attached ever since.

Now almost two years after starting the process, I have a perfect set of teeth and a beautiful smile :-)

I am happier, definitely healthier, and all thanks to Dr. Lanzon and Dr. Oquist. I highly recommend them whether you are just doing a small procedure or going for a complete dental replacement. They are well qualified, but more importantly they care about you and your smile. If I had to do it over again, I would choose them and am happy to recommend their services to anyone who is in need of excellent dental care.

B. John< /Text><Date>1567025267834</Date>< rating>

< Review>
Dr. Kaw is professional family doctor with friendly and professional staff. He is knowledgeable, caring and has a great bedside manner.<//Review>
</record>
</dataset><record>
< text>
I have been going to this spa for few months now and I think I am now ready to give my review.  I am sorry in advance that my review is pretty lengthy.

I have always been skeptical with new spas as they sprout everywhere, they come and go, and most of all, I have had bad experiences with a few. I used to go to a spa in Cerritos and then went with my esthetician that went freelancing after. Then my co-workers started raving about this new medical spa in Fullerton and I got so curious.  I finally went with some of friends and co-workers and oh my - I fell in love with The Retreat Medical Spa!

The ambiance is to die for, ultra-clean, comfortable, cozy, and luxurious. It is like walking into a high-end hotel. The hospitality of the staff is exemplary. I met the doctor who owns the place and then I was greeted with great smiles the staff and was offered their special house drink (which was apparently a recipe of the owner) and other refreshments - coffee, tea, etc.). I was then escorted to relax in their lounge, dimmed lights, cozy leather sofa, a selection of my favorite magazines. The ambiance was exhilarating and romantic - I wished that my husband was with me at that very moment.

I have had recent injection from Dr. Kaw. He made sure I understand the risk, benefits and side effects of my treatment. He made my injection so effortless, quick and with results that my friends are now so jealous of. Not to mention he has a very light touch.  I have referred more than ten friends to him since my injections.

Now lets talk about my facial treatment experience. As I mentioned earlier, I am very picky with my estheticians.  For the past few months, I have had both Amanda and Yvette, who are both very skillful and knowledgeable with the skin and esthetic skin products. They explain the steps of the treatment and answered my questions quite impressively. By the way, this medical spa uses both ZO Obagi and Skinmedica products that are high-end and expensive medical grade products. How do I know? Because I am a nurse, and I research anything that is used on my skin. Of course, they carry the same back bar products for purchase but they are not pushy at all to sell. I also tried their algae peel-off mask from Spain and it was heavenly soothing.

I also have had few massages there from Martin, Jessica and Jenny. They have different techniques but I enjoyed either one of them when I had my deep tissue and trigger point massage therapies.  I was skeptical at first to have a male massage therapist but because I know the owner of the spa is a medical doctor, I felt at ease that he would have screened his staff carefully. True enough, Martin was very professional.

A splendor of beauty and skillful staff describes my now routine monthly "retreat" at this spa. I now call this place my second home because my skin always feel rejuvenated. I also find joy and peace with the solemnity of the place and the hospitality of the staff.<//text>

< text>
Always an easy experience. Always trying to keep the lines down and moving fast. Great selection and helpful staff. It's been my go to grocery store ever since I moved to Napa.

****edited post renovation****
The new renovations completed beginning of 2020 are great. This Lucky now has a self serve salad and hot bar with many options for a quick lunch or dinner. There is seating at the front of the store if you want to eat your food before you leave.Their new frozen entre self serve option seems quite interesting although I have not tried it yet. As always the shelves are neat and faced and full of stock. Lucky prices are higher than other groceries but the shopping experience is above and beyond its competition and, I believe, worth paying a few extra pennies for!</text>
